## üîç Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### üéØ Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 45 page(s) - 45 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R4: Page has a descriptive title](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r4)
**Issue**: The `lang` attribute is either missing, empty, or only whitespace

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<html>...</html>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/html
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/html')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://my.northtyneside.gov.uk/
- https://www.northwarks.gov.uk/
- https://www.nuneatonandbedworth.gov.uk/
- https://www.oldham.gov.uk/
- https://www.oxford.gov.uk/
- *...and 40 more page(s)*

---

#### Pattern 2: Affects 32 page(s) - 32 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [region](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/region?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate
**Issue**: All page content should be contained by landmarks

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<center><h1>403 Forbidden</h1></center>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
center
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('center')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:

- https://www.nuneatonandbedworth.gov.uk/
- https://www.oldham.gov.uk/

#### Pattern 4: Affects 31 page(s) - 31 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [html-has-lang](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/html-has-lang?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious
**Issue**: <html> element must have a lang attribute

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<html><head><title>403 Forbidden</title></head>
<body>
<center><h1>403 Forbidden</h1></center>








</body></html>
```

```
html
```

#### Pattern 9: Affects 7 page(s) - 7 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**Issue**: Target has insufficient size

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<a id="ccc-info-link" class="ccc-link ccc-tabbable" href="https://www.civicuk.com/cookie-control" target="_blank" rel="noopener">...</a>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/a[@id="ccc-info-link"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/a[@id="ccc-info-link"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

#### Pattern 12: Affects 6 page(s) - 6 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [meta-refresh](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/meta-refresh?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical
**Issue**: Delayed refresh under 20 hours must not be used

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<meta http-equiv="refresh" content="360">
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
meta[http-equiv="refresh"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('meta[http-equiv="refresh"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Failure 1:**

- HTML: `<p class="govuk-body">We use some essential cookies to make this website...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="govuk-body"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="govuk-body govuk-body-s govuk-!-text-align-right search-disclaimer">AI-generated content can sometimes make mistakes. ...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="govuk-body govuk-body-s govuk-!-text-align-right search-disclaimer"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="govuk-body-s hp-links">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="govuk-body-s hp-links"]`

- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5

- XPath: `/p[@class="govuk-!-text-align-left govuk-!-margin-0"]`

**Failure 5:**

- XPath: `/a`

- Message: Target has insufficient size

- XPath: `/a[@class="menu__link"]`

## Detailed Failure Information (axe)

### https://www.ne-derbyshire.gov.uk/

#### Rule: [meta-refresh](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/meta-refresh?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Delayed refresh under 20 hours must not be used
- HTML: `<meta http-equiv="refresh" content="360">`
- XPath: `meta[http-equiv="refresh"]`

### https://www.north-herts.gov.uk/

#### Rule: [image-alt](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/image-alt?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img loading="lazy" src="/sites/default/files/styles/3_2_landscape_465x310/public/media-uploads/Stevenage%20Road.jpg?itok=bZqhfn0X" width="465" height="310" typeof="foaf:Image">`
- XPath: `.chevron-card:nth-child(1) > .views-field-field-listing-image.views-field > .field-content > a[hreflang="en"] > img[loading="lazy"][width="465"][height="310"]`

#### Rule: [landmark-no-duplicate-banner](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-no-duplicate-banner?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Document should not have more than one banner landmark
- HTML: `<div data-sitewide-alert="" role="banner"></div>`
- XPath: `div[data-sitewide-alert=""]`

#### Rule: [landmark-unique](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-unique?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Landmarks should have a unique role or role/label/title (i.e. accessible name) combination
- HTML: `<div data-sitewide-alert="" role="banner"></div>`
- XPath: `div[data-sitewide-alert=""]`

#### Rule: [link-name](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/link-name?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Links must have discernible text
- HTML: `<a href="/news/two-hitchin-streets-given-clean-air-clearance-after-council-decision" hreflang="en"><img loading="lazy" src="/sites/default/files/styles/3_2_landscape_465x310/public/media-uploads/Stevenage%20Road.jpg?itok=bZqhfn0X" width="465" height="310" typeof="foaf:Image">  </a>`
- XPath: `.chevron-card:nth-child(1) > .views-field-field-listing-image.views-field > .field-content > a[hreflang="en"]`

### https://www.northlincs.gov.uk/

#### Rule: [heading-order](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/heading-order?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Heading levels should only increase by one
- HTML: `<h5 class="card-title"><a href="https://www.northlincs.gov.uk/news/budget-2026-community-leisure-and-culture-projects-get-backing-in-budget/">Budget 2026: Community leisure and culture projects get backing...</a></h5>`
- XPath: `.col-md-4:nth-child(1) > .card.bg-light-grey.mb-3 > .card-body > h5`

### https://www.north-norfolk.gov.uk/

#### Rule: [aria-dialog-name](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-dialog-name?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: ARIA dialog and alertdialog nodes should have an accessible name
- HTML: `<div id="ccc-module" class="ccc-module--slideout ccc-module--left" role="dialog">`
- XPath: `#ccc-module`

#### Rule: [aria-required-children](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-required-children?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Certain ARIA roles must contain particular children
- HTML: `<div class="taskbar" id="taskbar" role="menu">`
- XPath: `#taskbar`

#### Rule: [aria-required-parent](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-required-parent?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Certain ARIA roles must be contained by particular parents
- HTML: `<li role="menuitemradio" class="taskbar-link" aria-checked="false">                 <a href="/task-tags/task-types/pay/" data-id="1105" data-name="Pay" title="List of Pay Type Tasks">                     Pay                 </a>             </li>`
- XPath: `.taskbar-link[role="menuitemradio"]:nth-child(1)`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Certain ARIA roles must be contained by particular parents
- HTML: `<li role="menuitemradio" class="taskbar-link" aria-checked="false">                 <a href="/task-tags/task-types/report/" data-id="1108" data-name="Report" title="List of Report Type Tasks">                     Report                 </a>             </li>`
- XPath: `.taskbar-link[role="menuitemradio"]:nth-child(2)`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Certain ARIA roles must be contained by particular parents
- HTML: `<li role="menuitemradio" class="taskbar-link" aria-checked="false">                 <a href="/task-tags/task-types/apply/" data-id="1109" data-name="Apply" title="List of Apply Type Tasks">                     Apply                 </a>             </li>`
- XPath: `.taskbar-link[role="menuitemradio"]:nth-child(3)`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Certain ARIA roles must be contained by particular parents
- HTML: `<li role="menuitemradio" class="taskbar-link" aria-checked="false">                 <a href="/task-tags/task-types/view/" data-id="1111" data-name="View" title="List of View Type Tasks">                     View                 </a>             </li>`
- XPath: `.taskbar-link[role="menuitemradio"]:nth-child(4)`

#### Rule: [landmark-banner-is-top-level](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-banner-is-top-level?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Banner landmark should not be contained in another landmark
- HTML: `<div class="global-header" role="banner" aria-label="Website Header">`
- XPath: `.global-header`

#### Rule: [landmark-no-duplicate-banner](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-no-duplicate-banner?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Document should not have more than one banner landmark
- HTML: `<header>`
- XPath: `.wrapper > header`

#### Rule: [list](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/list?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: <ul> and <ol> must only directly contain <li>, <script> or <template> elements
- HTML: `<ul class="taskbar-navigation-list">`
- XPath: `.taskbar-navigation-list`

#### Rule: [nested-interactive](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/nested-interactive?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Interactive controls must not be nested

- XPath: `#search-popup`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<div>`
- XPath: `body > div:nth-child(10)`

**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements should not have tabindex greater than zero
- HTML: `<a href="#main" accesskey="s" tabindex="1">Skip to content</a>`
- XPath: `a[href$="#main"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Elements should not have tabindex greater than zero
- HTML: `<a tabindex="1" href="#" data-id="cookie-accept" class="btn btn-primary"> Accept</a>`
- XPath: `a[data-id="cookie-accept"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Elements should not have tabindex greater than zero
- HTML: `<a tabindex="1" href="#" data-id="cookie-manage" class="btn btn-secondary"> Manage cookies</a>`
- XPath: `.btn-secondary`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Elements should not have tabindex greater than zero
- HTML: `<button data-id="cookie-close" type="button" tabindex="1">             <span class="icon-close"></span>             <span class="visually-hidden">Hide this notice</span>         </button>`
- XPath: `button[data-id="cookie-close"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Elements should not have tabindex greater than zero
- HTML: `<a tabindex="1" href="/" class="logo" aria-label="Islington for a more equal future, Islington Council logo, Islington council home page"><img src="/_common/img/svg/fallback/logo.png" alt="Islington for a more equal future, Islington Council logo, Islington council home page"></a>`
- XPath: `.m-header-inner > .logo[href="/"]`
